>会引燃易燃物，并且对区域内的物品造成伤害。它可以熔化低熔点的金属，例如铅、金、铜、银、青铜。如果伤害足以粉碎或破坏这类阻碍，火球术可以扩散到这阻碍后；否则和其他法术效果一样，它会被这阻碍所阻止。</font></span><span >施法者举起一只手，璀璨夺目的白色光球出现在张开的手掌前方，随后化为横掠天际的耀眼白色光焰，向目标轰击。使用施法检定进行远程接触攻击（忽视护甲和天生防御），这次攻击的每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10kg/</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >智力值的物品。你每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >智力上的附加成功，可以指定一个人在此道路上行走。这条道路可以在空中任意扭曲起伏转折，但你必须依正常规则行走于其上。道路的两面都是有可能行走的。你可以在施法的同时决定道路的走向，若你不如此做，道路将自动在你面前半米处向前伸展，并随时随你的心意出现起伏或转弯。但道路一旦出现，就不可改变。一旦道路长度用完，则前方向前延伸的同时尾部会等速消失。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span >威力值的速度飞行，机动性为良好。使用飞行术和在地面上行走一样，不需要额外的专注，因此受术者可以正常的攻击或施法。飞行术的受术者可以冲锋但不能奔跑，他的携带重量也不能超过它最大负重。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span >米。如果在此期间内他接触到了地面，那么他将安全着陆。如果没有，他会从剩余的高度处跌落。由于解除一个魔法实际上就是结束它，因此如果飞行术被解除掉，受术者依然可以以这种方式下降。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >要使用这道法术，施法者必须先进行一次施法检定，并具有威力值的增强加值，与其他来源的增强加值叠加。欲击破的防御若为法术，则对抗对方的施法检定；若为其他超自然能力，则对方以展现能力的检定对抗；若对方能力不需检定，则投意志。你每胜出</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你可以将自己体内的时间加速，一切周围的事物对你都显得缓慢下来。在启动这道法术时，你同时需要决定其倍率，上限为每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >4</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点威力值一倍。之后，你因所加速的每一倍在敏捷相关检定上获得</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+4DP</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >和</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >附加成功，同时速度增加</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >米，这些均为速度加值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你也可以用这个法术来减缓自己体内的时间。当如此使用这道法术时，你体内的时间倍速变为反比例减缓，并改为带来等量的速度减值。基于当前的倍速，这个用法可以降低你在呼吸，心跳上的生理特征，所有创伤、毒素和疾病来源的效果对你的影响同比例降低，但持续时间相应延长。对于针对人类的振动探测而言，你不视为人类。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >当法术效果结束时，世界的修正会回到你的身上。你以这个法术所篡改的每一倍时间流速都会让你受到</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点不可吸收的冲击伤害。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：你可以用额外支付</font></span><span >炼金师们在研究生命与人体之迷时找到了这种可怕的药物，它可以透过肉体作用于生物的精神与灵魂，用虚妄的快感破坏他们的生存意志，比任何毒品都更强大。善用时，它是一种称手而可怕的工具。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >在炼制的过程中，你需要进行一次施法检定，以决定这道法术的效果。当你炼制完成时，你得到了一剂</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >毫升如水状无色无臭的溶液。这溶液有三种使用方式：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >、你可以用此液体直接攻击生物，这是一次投掷攻击，如同接触攻击一般无视天生防御和护甲防御，但不造成任何伤害，此外，伤害减免对这次攻击同样无法奏效。若攻击命中，它可以从生物的体表渗入。一剂溶液对一个生物生效，该生物投意志对抗你的施法成功数，每失败</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1 </span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >则承受</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点晕眩点数。若该生物因此进入昏迷状态，它醒来后对迷情水上瘾，必须经过一个</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >为威力值的意志检定，若失败，则它会强烈渴望再次使用迷情水。该判定每天进行一次，每次成功都会使</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >－</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。每次失败后若使用迷情水，则</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >＋</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >。若你使生物服用或饮下全部迷情水，则昏迷时间和上瘾</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >DC</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >都加倍，但食盐、银制品或任何高于</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;80</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&#8451;的温度都会破坏迷情水的作用。</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >、你可以将一剂迷情水稀释</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍，用作</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >副兴奋剂。当你因巨大痛苦或疲劳效果而承受减值时，饮用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >副此兴奋剂，可以忽略相当于威力值的减值。但饮用兴奋剂同样会上瘾。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >、若将稀释</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >10</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >倍的迷情水雾化，它可以充斥</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >米半径的球形扩散区域。皮肤或身体表面接触到雾化迷情水的生物会承受等于威力值的晕眩点数，持续轮数相当于你的施法成功数。他们可以通过成功的意志对抗使晕眩点数降为</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点。在封闭空间中，此雾会持续</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >轮，在开阔空间中雾化迷情水会持续</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >轮，之后耗散殆尽。你可以使用雾化液体的法术、能力甚至仅仅通过喷雾器来雾化迷情水。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >ST</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：无</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >掌握暗之魔法的证明，也是暗之魔法的基础形态。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >在这个形态下，你能认识到暗的本质，理解，接纳，包容，直到吞噬。你双手手背到小臂的变黑色，并且浮现出美丽的白色花纹，这视同一个概念武装。启动此概念武装是一个自由动作，启动后只要没有关闭过，为维持而支付魔力不视为第二次启动。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >暗夜之型</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >每启动一次，都会造成</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点不可吸收减免的严重伤害的明伤，这个伤害在恢复时难度视为恶性伤害对待。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >暗夜之型</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >每启动一次，还会造成</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点不可吸收减免的严重伤害的暗伤，这个伤害不会立刻显现，而是暗中累积，这个伤害累积的总数超过人物的耐力值时，该次暗夜之型结束人物会陷入</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >8</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >小时的昏迷，之后这个伤害清空。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >+2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >使魔与魔术师有着肉体上和精神上的联系，所以使魔即魔术师的分身。魔术师大都躲在家中不外出，埋首于魔术研究中，少理凡尘俗事；于是出外收集情报、调度材料等杂务，就都交由这个分身处理。随着在外活动而成长，使魔慢慢就成为象征魔术师的存在。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施展这道法术时，首先利用小动物的尸骸作容器，注入他人的残留思念生成人格，制造出拟似生命；再加上魔术师身体存有魔术回路的一部份，如血、头发、眼等作为肉体的联系，因而每只使魔都会占用</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点魔力上限，并消耗</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点经验值。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >当这道法术被完成后，你获得一个体积</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >以下的生物做为你的使魔，它的生理属性和感官如同它活着的时候，心智属性和社交属性使用你本人的。另外，使魔的外表如同它生前的模样，但某些手段可以侦测到它身上的魔力波动。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >你可以与它共享知觉并且控制它，共享使魔的知觉或对它下达命令是一个自由动作。除此以外，若你在施展接触性法术时它在你的触及范围内，你可以让它为你传递暂不散发的法术效果。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >虽然有殖入魔术回路，但由于没有生成魔力的机能，使魔必须依赖魔术师的魔力维生，失去主人的使魔便无法独自活下去。在第一次完成使魔的制作时，以及之后的每一天你都需要为每只使魔补充</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >3</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >感知，超过此距离则无法传递魔力、法术和命令。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >个场景（可解消）</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-weight:bold;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >对抗</font></span></b><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >：无</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >为了得到安宁和平静，御术师们召唤了古木的灵魂，在空间中构建出无尽丛林的虚影，这就是万叶冥响。树魂会吸收和解消一切不安与动乱，保护范围内所有生灵。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >施展</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >万叶冥想</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >，你需要有画下魔法阵的介质，以及一个大约一尺见方的平面用于画阵。在你施法完成时，以你为中心，法术范围内会出现古木丛林的幻影，高耸千尺。千年树魂会吸收对范围内造成不安的能量，带来如下效果：</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><br></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >范围内所有生物免疫低于法术等级的影响心灵、意志或灵魂的效果，并在对抗此类效果时受到加值，等同于你施法判定的成功数，但不超过威力值。已经被这一类能力所危害的生物立刻获得一次对抗或免疫的机会。范围内的生物所具有的所有士气加值或减值因此暂时无效，但它可以通过一个成功的意志对抗拒绝接受</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >万叶冥想</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >赋予的心灵免疫能力。对于范围内的每一个与法术等级同级或更低的诅咒效果，你以施法判定对抗其展现判定，若你成功，可以将诅咒的效果暂时压制到</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >万叶冥响</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >结束，若你胜出</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >5</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >或更多，你可以解除这一诅咒。在此范围内的生物无法使用意志力，另外，</font></span><i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-style:italic;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >万叶冥响</font></span></i><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >为每个生物提供每</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >2</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >威力值</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >1</span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" ><font face="宋体" >点全伤害吸收。</font></span><span style="mso-spacerun:'yes';font-family:Calibri;mso-fareast-font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;font-size:10.0000pt;mso-font-kerning:0.0000pt;" >&nbsp;</span><span
